< review>
One thing that confused me when arriving at the facility is that it‚Äôs inside the big office building with the parking garage underneath it. I could see a sign with Advance sleep on it so I had to check the address again and make sure I was at the right place. It actually worked out to be better than I expected because it‚Äôs quite a secure location. You access the office from the elevator in the parking garage if your there after hours! On the wall beside it there are instructions on how to use the elevator because it is locked and requires a passcode. When I finally made it to the office I was greeted by Michael who was my Respiratory Therapist. He was welcoming and friendly and showed me to my room for the night. In the room there is basically everything you would have in a hotel room (except the minibar!!) The room was cozy and clean. The wires were all laid out on the bed so after getting changed into pjs I sat in a chair where Michael attached all the wires to my head, legs and chest. He was easy to talk to and super friendly. It made me feel much less anxious. There is a bathroom with a shower, sink, toilet and plenty of room to change. It‚Äôs very clean and nicely decorated. After laying in bed and after Michael had calibrated the wires and machines I was able to either watch tv, read or use my phone until I was sleepy. You have a call button and you can press it if you need assistance during the night. It was easy to detach me from the wall so I could use the restroom if I needed it. The bed in the room could have been a little more comfortable but it‚Äôs only for one night and the sheets were very clean and soft so it wasn‚Äôt a big deal. After the night is done, I was woken at 5am to be detached from the wires and after you‚Äôre unhooked you can leave. It was such a smooth process and not as worrying as I had thought. There are quite a few other bedrooms in the facility so you can sometimes hear noises but it wasn‚Äôt a problem either. I would definitely recommend this sleep study center. And Michael gets 5 stars from me!</review>

Horrible!  The woman who checked me in and got me set up was 5 star, but the experience in the morning was so bad, I wish I could give this zero stars.  There was NO advance notice that they would be waking us patients up at FIVE AM and kicking us out by 5:30!  (I don't drive due to disability and I had told my driver I'd be done around 8. I had filled out a survey before going and I said I normally went to bed around 11~12, so I assumed they'd want 8 hours of sleep data.)  The pre~visit email they sent said patients would be following our normal sleep routines...so how is going lights out around 10:30, falling asleep maybe 2 hours later, and waking many times from the uncomfortable sleep apnea mask then being woken at 5 ~ in all getting maybe 2 hours of sleep ~ following our normal routine???  People going for sleep studies normally have horrid insomnia, so why on earth would you wake them at FIVE AM???  I sometimes don't even fall asleep until after 4am!  (But I had purposely not slept at all the previous 2 nights to ensure I'd fall asleep while at the sleep clinic, but if I hadn't done that, I would have had an hour or less of sleep!)  When the male attendant woke me in the morning, I tried to explain that my ride wasn't coming for 3 more hours and he could care less. He told me I couldn't go back to sleep, must dress immediately and get out.  When I repeated I could not leave because I had no where to go, he was rude.  He wouldn't let me remain safe inside their lobby awaiting my ride, said he was going home and wouldn't be forced to do overtime for me and made me leave the office.  I sat for three hours in the freezing cold on an uncomfortable bench in the public lobby of an office building ~ with (I hadn't realized at the time I was rushed out of their office because I was dead tired) blobs of white glue all over my face and in my hair from the electrotrodes.  It wasn't until I got home and looked in the mirror that I realized what I looked like and that explained why 3 people entering the building to work around 7:30 questioned me as to what I was doing in their lobby ~ I looked like a homeless person sitting there with my overnight bag, my hair in clumps and white stuff all over my face.  Humiliating!  And, the attendant could have let me stay in their private office lobby for quite a while instead of kicking me out at 5:30.  I did not hear him leave until 7:20!  I can't believe my medical insurance paid a ton of money for this kind of service and for getting maybe 2 hours of sleep data.  One of the main reason I was sent to the sleep clinic was because I had unsuccessfully tried 2 different sleep apnea machines at home (one for 5 nights and the other for 7 nights) and could not fall asleep with them because the strength of the blowing air was too strong/uncomfortable and I felt like I was choking and couldn't exhale.  My doctor said he wanted me at the sleep clinic so they could adjust settings in real time, rather than seeing the data the following morning and re~setting things for the next night.  But when the air pressure ramped up and woke me up because it was getting hard to breath and was lifting the mask off my face, instead of adjusting settings, finding one I could sleep with, the man just tightened the mask (twice).  So after all that, we still don't know what the proper setting are that will allow me to sleep without waking feeling like I can't breathe.   Oh, and when you have a lovely female nurse set you up and put you to sleep, you should be informed (warned?) that someone else may be taking care of you later.  I was quite shocked when I woke in the night and used my call button that a man I had never seen before and was not told may be assisting me later entered my room to help me and didn't even introduce himself.  Since this is an odd, uncomfortable process, it would be nice to have the same technician/nurse from night until morning, or at least be introduced to anyone new who may be entering your room in the dark.</review>

<Date>1613071465076<//Date><rating>5< /rating><Text>All of the employees are always so friendly. They actually act like human beings, instead of standing at the register like robots at other places saying "Can I take your order" without even looking at you. Even the employees in the back making the food say "Hi" and will chat a bit with you. They are fast as heck too! It doesn't matter if you order over the phone, online, or in person, you get the same fast, courteous service with a smile. I've ordered in person several times, and waited outside while they make it. While outside, the drivers will even stop, say "Hi" and chat. I was surprised each time when someone brought my order out to me, instead of having it sit inside waiting for me to wonder if it was ready yet or not and go inside to get it. That's great customer service! Oh, and the sausage really tastes like....Sausage LOL! The Papadias are yummy! I love all of their pizzas, but I'm hooked on the Canadian bacon and pineapple with Alfredo sauce instead of red sauce. And don't forget to get the stuffed crust, it's seriously cheesy! They always have great prices and specials too. Go in, and watch them hand toss and spin the dough while you're waiting, It's fun! <rating>5<//rating>< review>
The Fleet Feet Sports Shoes in Stockton is a great store. Briana helped me find the right inserts for my shoes. I went in for orthopedic inserts, and ended up buying shoes too. I'm on my feet a lot at work, and need  support. Briana did an in-dept examination of my feet. From how I walk, my gait, my arches, and sized my foot. I didn't realize what good shoes look like. I've been buying the wrong type of shoes. I've been going through shoes, because they'd feel good for short walking in store, but at home I'd realize they would hurt my feet. There was no pressure in buying shoes. I now know what to look for in shoes, so when I purchase anymore shoes from a regular store  I will have better success. I also  bought these cute sunglasses. They have more then shoes. The specialize sports clothes, accessories,etc. A great experience with their knowledgeable staff. I was very impressed with my whole experience. I highly recommend this store. The inserts were cut and placed in my new shoes. The problem is once I left, the shoe was pressing on this bunion. I went back a few days later to get the 3/4 size of arch support and let them know that is what I needed. They took full responsibility and provided the correct insert. The other girl, I didn't get her name, placed the arch support under the shoes original padding, and that was a great idea. This allowed my foot to have more toe room. Fleets feet sports deducted the price of the one I originally bought with the new 3/4 inset. I didn't have to buy another insert, another sign of a good company. The only recommendation would be to order customer shoes, not every other Monday.< /review>

I took my son Julius into Fleet Feet Sports in Stockton as he's embarking on his first year on the high school cross country team as a freshman coming into Lincoln High School.  First thing that was cool was that one of his coaches works at the store so we knew we'd get service that mattered.  We were not disappointed at all, and his coach wasn't even the one that helped us.

Julius tried on several pairs of shoes including brands that were not so main stream like Nike and Adidas.  We had his foot measured for exact fit and the whole experience from beginning to end lasted about 20-25 minutes.  We were not ignored throughout the experience, so that means we received 20-25 minutes of total attention.  Julius immediately fell in love with the shoes we chose and all is good.

We also looked at other running specific items in the store for the future and we now know this is the location in Stockton to purchase from for serious runners.

Thanks Fleet Feet!</text>
